Cholera	B-Disease

.	O
''	O

Equine	B-Virus
infectious	I-Virus
anemia	I-Virus
is	O
a	O
viral	O
disease	O
that	O
attacks	O
horses	O
'	O
immune	O
systems	O
.	O

The	O
virus	O
is	O
transmitted	O
through	O

exchange	O
of	O
body	O

from	O
an	O
infected	O

animal	O

often	O

,	O

more	O

through	O
the	O
use	O
of	O

instruments	O
or	O
needles	O
.	O

A	O
Coggins	O
test	O
screens	O
horses	O
'	O
blood	O
for	O
antibodies	O
that	O
are	O

of	O

.	O

.	O
